cd /testbed && cat > test_json_fix.cs << 'EOF'
using System;
using System.Text.Json.Nodes;
using Orleans.Serialization;
using Microsoft.Extensions.DependencyInjection;
using System.Text.Json;

namespace TestJsonFix
{
    class Program
    {
        static void Main(string[] args)
        {
            // Create service provider with JSON serialization
            var services = new ServiceCollection();
            services.AddSerializer(serializerBuilder =>
            {
                serializerBuilder.AddJsonSerializer();
            });
            
            var serviceProvider = services.BuildServiceProvider();
            var serializer = serviceProvider.GetRequiredService<Serializer>();
            
            // Test case: JsonValue created with int (the problematic case from the PR)
            var jsonValue = JsonValue.Create(1);
            Console.WriteLine("Original type: " + jsonValue.GetType());
            Console.WriteLine("Value: " + jsonValue);
            
            try
            {
                // Serialize and deserialize
                var serialized = serializer.Serialize(jsonValue);
                var deserialized = serializer.Deserialize(serialized);
                
                Console.WriteLine("Deserialized type: " + deserialized?.GetType());
                Console.WriteLine("Deserialized value: " + deserialized);
                
                // Test if we can cast to JsonValue (this was failing before)
                if (deserialized is JsonValue deserializedValue)
                {
                    Console.WriteLine("Cast to JsonValue successful");
                    Console.WriteLine("Extracted value: " + deserializedValue.GetValue<object>());
                }
                
                Console.WriteLine("SUCCESS: No exception occurred");
            }
            catch (InvalidCastException ex)
            {
                Console.WriteLine("INVALID CAST ERROR: " + ex.Message);
            }
            catch (Exception ex)
            {
                Console.WriteLine("OTHER ERROR: " + ex.ToString());
            }
            
            // Test other JsonValue types
            Console.WriteLine("\n=== Testing other JsonValue types ===");
            TestJsonValue(JsonValue.Create(true));
            TestJsonValue(JsonValue.Create("hello"));
            TestJsonValue(JsonValue.Create(3.14));
        }
        
        static void TestJsonValue(JsonValue value)
        {
            var services = new ServiceCollection();
            services.AddSerializer(serializerBuilder =>
            {
                serializerBuilder.AddJsonSerializer();
            });
            
            var serviceProvider = services.BuildServiceProvider();
            var serializer = serviceProvider.GetRequiredService<Serializer>();
            
            try
            {
                var serialized = serializer.Serialize(value);
                var deserialized = serializer.Deserialize(serialized);
                
                Console.WriteLine($"{value.GetType().Name} -> {deserialized?.GetType().Name}: Success");
                
                if (deserialized is JsonValue dv)
                {
                    Console.WriteLine($"  Value: {dv.GetValue<object>()}");
                }
            }
            catch (Exception ex)
            {
                Console.WriteLine($"{value.GetType().Name} -> ERROR: {ex.Message}");
            }
        }
    }
}
EOF

cd /testbed && cat > test_simple_fix.cs << 'EOF'
using System;
using System.Text.Json.Nodes;
using Orleans.Serialization;
using Microsoft.Extensions.DependencyInjection;

namespace TestSimpleFix
{
    class Program
    {
        static void Main(string[] args)
        {
            // Create service provider with JSON serialization
            var services = new ServiceCollection();
            services.AddSerializer(serializerBuilder =>
            {
                serializerBuilder.AddJsonSerializer();
            });
            
            var serviceProvider = services.BuildServiceProvider();
            var serializer = serviceProvider.GetRequiredService<Serializer>();
            
            // Test case: JsonValue created with int (the problematic case from the PR)
            var jsonValue = JsonValue.Create(1);
            Console.WriteLine("Original type: " + jsonValue.GetType());
            Console.WriteLine("Value: " + jsonValue);
            
            try
            {
                // Serialize and deserialize
                var serialized = serializer.Serialize(jsonValue);
                var deserialized = serializer.Deserialize(serialized);
                
                Console.WriteLine("Deserialized type: " + deserialized?.GetType());
                Console.WriteLine("Deserialized value: " + deserialized);
                
                // Test if we can cast to JsonValue (this was failing before)
                if (deserialized is JsonValue deserializedValue)
                {
                    Console.WriteLine("Cast to JsonValue successful");
                    Console.WriteLine("Extracted value: " + deserializedValue.GetValue<object>());
                }
                
                Console.WriteLine("SUCCESS: No exception occurred");
            }
            catch (InvalidCastException ex)
            {
                Console.WriteLine("INVALID CAST ERROR: " + ex.Message);
                Console.WriteLine("This indicates the fix did not work properly");
            }
            catch (Exception ex)
            {
                Console.WriteLine("OTHER ERROR: " + ex.ToString());
            }
            
            // Test grain method parameter scenario
            Console.WriteLine("\n=== Testing grain method parameter scenario ===");
            TestGrainScenario();
        }
        
        static void TestGrainScenario()
        {
            // Simulate what happens when a grain method with JsonNode parameter is called
            var services = new ServiceCollection();
            services.AddSerializer(serializerBuilder =>
            {
                serializerBuilder.AddJsonSerializer();
            });
            
            var serviceProvider = services.BuildServiceProvider();
            var serializer = serviceProvider.GetRequiredService<Serializer>();
            
            // This simulates: grain.InvokeAsync(JsonValue.Create(1))
            var parameter = JsonValue.Create(1);
            
            try
            {
                // Serialize the parameter
                var serializedParam = serializer.Serialize(parameter);
                
                // Deserialize as JsonNode (what the grain method expects)
                var deserializedParam = serializer.Deserialize(serializedParam);
                
                Console.WriteLine("Parameter type: " + parameter.GetType());
                Console.WriteLine("Deserialized parameter type: " + deserializedParam?.GetType());
                
                // Try to use it as JsonNode (this should work now)
                if (deserializedParam is JsonNode node)
                {
                    Console.WriteLine("Successfully cast to JsonNode");
                    Console.WriteLine("Node value: " + node);
                }
                
                Console.WriteLine("GRAIN SCENARIO: SUCCESS");
            }
            catch (InvalidCastException ex)
            {
                Console.WriteLine("GRAIN SCENARIO FAILED: " + ex.Message);
            }
        }
    }
}
EOF

using System;
using System.Text.Json.Nodes;
using Orleans.Serialization.SystemTextJson;
using Microsoft.Extensions.DependencyInjection;

namespace TestSimpleFix
{
    class Program
    {
        static void Main(string[] args)
        {
            Console.WriteLine("=== Testing JsonValue serialization fix ===\n");
            
            // Create service provider with JSON serialization
            var services = new ServiceCollection();
            services.AddSerializer()
                .AddJsonSerializer(isSupportedType: type => typeof(JsonNode).IsAssignableFrom(type));
            
            var serviceProvider = services.BuildServiceProvider();
            var serializer = serviceProvider.GetRequiredService<Serializer>();
            
            // Test case: JsonValue created with int (the problematic case from the PR)
            var jsonValue = JsonValue.Create(1);
            Console.WriteLine("Original type: " + jsonValue.GetType());
            Console.WriteLine("Value: " + jsonValue);
            
            try
            {
                // Serialize and deserialize
                var serialized = serializer.SerializeToArray(jsonValue);
                var deserialized = serializer.Deserialize(serialized);
                
                Console.WriteLine("Deserialized type: " + deserialized?.GetType());
                Console.WriteLine("Deserialized value: " + deserialized);
                
                // Test if we can cast to JsonValue (this was failing before)
                if (deserialized is JsonValue deserializedValue)
                {
                    Console.WriteLine("Cast to JsonValue successful");
                    Console.WriteLine("Extracted value: " + deserializedValue.GetValue<object>());
                }
                
                Console.WriteLine("SUCCESS: No exception occurred");
            }
            catch (InvalidCastException ex)
            {
                Console.WriteLine("INVALID CAST ERROR: " + ex.Message);
                Console.WriteLine("This indicates the fix did not work properly");
            }
            catch (Exception ex)
            {
                Console.WriteLine("OTHER ERROR: " + ex.ToString());
            }
        }
    }
}

        [Fact]
        public void CanSerializeNativeJsonTypes()
        {
            JsonArray jsonArray = new JsonArray([JsonValue.Create(true), JsonValue.Create(42), JsonValue.Create("hello")]);
            JsonObject? jsonObject = System.Text.Json.JsonSerializer.Deserialize<JsonObject>("{\"foo\": \"bar\"}");

            var deserializedArray = RoundTripThroughUntypedSerializer(jsonArray, out _);
            Assert.Equal(System.Text.Json.JsonSerializer.Serialize(jsonArray), System.Text.Json.JsonSerializer.Serialize(deserializedArray));

            var deserializedObject = RoundTripThroughUntypedSerializer(jsonObject, out _);
            Assert.Equal(System.Text.Json.JsonSerializer.Serialize(jsonObject), System.Text.Json.JsonSerializer.Serialize(deserializedObject));
        }
    }

+using System;
+using System.Text.Json.Nodes;
+using System.Text.Json;
+
+namespace AnalyzeJsonCodec
+{
+    class Program
+    {
+        static void Main(string[] args)
+        {
+            // The issue is in how Orleans JsonCodec handles JsonValue serialization
+            // When it serializes JsonValue.Create(1):
+            // - It stores the type as JsonValuePrimitive<int>
+            // - It serializes the value as JSON: 1
+            
+            // When deserializing:
+            // - It reads the stored type: JsonValuePrimitive<int>  
+            // - It tries to deserialize JSON: 1 to that type
+            // - But System.Text.Json.Deserialize with JsonValuePrimitive<int> doesn't work correctly
+            
+            Console.WriteLine("=== Analyzing the JsonCodec issue ===\n");
+            
+            // Test what happens when we try to deserialize directly to JsonValuePrimitive<int>
+            TestDirectDeserialization();
+            
+            // Test the workaround that Orleans should use
+            TestWorkaround();
+        }
+        
+        static void TestDirectDeserialization()
+        {
+            Console.WriteLine("=== Testing direct deserialization to JsonValuePrimitive<int> ===");
+            
+            var original = JsonValue.Create(1);
+            Console.WriteLine($"Original: {original.GetType()}");
+            
+            var json = JsonSerializer.Serialize(original);
+            Console.WriteLine($"JSON: {json}");
+            
+            // This is what Orleans JsonCodec tries to do
+            try
+            {
+                // Try to deserialize directly to the original type
+                var options = new JsonSerializerOptions();
+                var deserialized = JsonSerializer.Deserialize(json, original.GetType(), options);
+                Console.WriteLine($"Direct deserialization result: {deserialized?.GetType() ?? Type.GetType("null")}");
+                
+                if (deserialized != null)
+                {
+                    Console.WriteLine($"Value: {deserialized}");
+                }
+            }
+            catch (Exception ex)
+            {
+                Console.WriteLine($"DIRECT DESERIALIZATION FAILED: {ex.Message}");
+                Console.WriteLine($"Exception type: {ex.GetType()}");
+            }
+        }
+        
+        static void TestWorkaround()
+        {
+            Console.WriteLine("\n=== Testing workaround ===");
+            
+            var original = JsonValue.Create(1);
+            var json = JsonSerializer.Serialize(original);
+            
+            // The correct approach: deserialize to JsonNode first, then handle conversion
+            var deserializedNode = JsonSerializer.Deserialize<JsonNode>(json);
+            Console.WriteLine($"Deserialized as JsonNode: {deserializedNode?.GetType()}");
+            
+            // Now we need to convert it back to the original type
+            // The issue is that JsonValuePrimitive<JsonElement> != JsonValuePrimitive<int>
+            // but they both implement JsonValue and have the same underlying value
+            
+            if (deserializedNode is JsonValue jsonValue && jsonValue != null)
+            {
+                Console.WriteLine($"It's a JsonValue: {jsonValue.GetType()}");
+                
+                // Get the underlying value
+                var underlyingValue = jsonValue.GetValue<object>();
+                Console.WriteLine($"Underlying value: {underlyingValue} (type: {underlyingValue?.GetType()})");
+                
+                // We can recreate the original JsonValue by using JsonValue.Create with the underlying value
+                if (underlyingValue != null)
+                {
+                    var recreated = JsonValue.Create(underlyingValue);
+                    Console.WriteLine($"Recreated: {recreated?.GetType()}");
+                    
+                    // But this still won't be JsonValuePrimitive<int> if underlyingValue is JsonElement
+                    // We need to extract the actual value from JsonElement
+                    
+                    if (underlyingValue is JsonElement jsonElement)
+                    {
+                        Console.WriteLine("Underlying value is JsonElement, extracting actual value...");
+                        
+                        object? actualValue = ExtractValueFromJsonElement(jsonElement);
+                        
+                        Console.WriteLine($"Extracted actual value: {actualValue} (type: {actualValue?.GetType()})");
+                        
+                        if (actualValue != null)
+                        {
+                            var properlyRecreated = JsonValue.Create(actualValue);
+                            Console.WriteLine($"Properly recreated: {properlyRecreated?.GetType()}");
+                            
+                            // Compare with original
+                            Console.WriteLine($"Original: {original.GetType()}");
+                            Console.WriteLine($"Match: {properlyRecreated?.GetType() == original.GetType()}");
+                        }
+                    }
+                }
+            }
+        }
+        
+        static object? ExtractValueFromJsonElement(JsonElement element)
+        {
+            return element.ValueKind switch
+            {
+                JsonValueKind.Number when element.TryGetInt32(out int intValue) => intValue,
+                JsonValueKind.Number when element.TryGetInt64(out long longValue) => longValue,
+                JsonValueKind.Number when element.TryGetDouble(out double doubleValue) => doubleValue,
+                JsonValueKind.True => true,
+                JsonValueKind.False => false,
+                JsonValueKind.String => element.GetString(),
+                JsonValueKind.Null => null,
+                _ => element // fallback
+            };
+        }
+    }
+}

+using System;
+using System.Text.Json.Nodes;
+
+namespace SimpleTest
+{
+    class Program
+    {
+        static void Main(string[] args)
+        {
+            // Test the JsonValue creation and type information
+            var jsonValue = JsonValue.Create(1);
+            Console.WriteLine("JsonValue type: " + jsonValue.GetType().FullName);
+            Console.WriteLine("JsonValue is JsonValue: " + (jsonValue is JsonValue));
+            Console.WriteLine("JsonValue is JsonNode: " + (jsonValue is JsonNode));
+            
+            // Check if it's a specific generic type
+            var valueType = jsonValue.GetType();
+            Console.WriteLine("Is generic type: " + valueType.IsGenericType);
+            if (valueType.IsGenericType)
+            {
+                Console.WriteLine("Generic type definition: " + valueType.GetGenericTypeDefinition());
+                Console.WriteLine("Generic arguments: " + string.Join(", ", valueType.GetGenericArguments()));
+            }
+            
+            // Test serialization directly with System.Text.Json
+            var jsonString = System.Text.Json.JsonSerializer.Serialize(jsonValue);
+            Console.WriteLine("Serialized JSON: " + jsonString);
+            
+            // Try to deserialize back to JsonNode type
+            var deserialized = System.Text.Json.JsonSerializer.Deserialize<JsonNode>(jsonString);
+            Console.WriteLine("Deserialized type: " + deserialized.GetType().FullName);
+            
+            // Try deserializing to specific JsonValue type
+            try
+            {
+                var deserializedValue = System.Text.Json.JsonSerializer.Deserialize<JsonValue>(jsonString);
+                Console.WriteLine("Deserialized JsonValue type: " + deserializedValue.GetType().FullName);
+            }
+            catch (Exception ex)
+            {
+                Console.WriteLine("Error deserializing to JsonValue: " + ex.Message);
+            }
+        }
+    }

+using System;
+using System.Text.Json.Nodes;
+using System.Text.Json;
+
+namespace TestJsonIssue
+{
+    class Program
+    {
+        static void Main(string[] args)
+        {
+            // Simulate what Orleans serialization does
+            var jsonValue = JsonValue.Create(1);
+            Console.WriteLine("Original type: " + jsonValue.GetType());
+            
+            // Serialize
+            var options = new JsonSerializerOptions();
+            var jsonBytes = JsonSerializer.SerializeToUtf8Bytes(jsonValue, options);
+            Console.WriteLine("Serialized: " + System.Text.Encoding.UTF8.GetString(jsonBytes));
+            
+            // Try to deserialize back to JsonNode
+            try
+            {
+                var readerOptions = new JsonReaderOptions();
+                var reader = new Utf8JsonReader(jsonBytes, readerOptions);
+                var deserialized = JsonSerializer.Deserialize<JsonNode>(ref reader, options);
+                Console.WriteLine("Deserialized type: " + deserialized?.GetType());
+                Console.WriteLine("SUCCESS: No exception");
+            }
+            catch (Exception ex)
+            {
+                Console.WriteLine("ERROR: " + ex);
+            }
+            
+            // Try to deserialize back to JsonValue
+            try
+            {
+                var readerOptions = new JsonReaderOptions();
+                var reader = new Utf8JsonReader(jsonBytes, readerOptions);
+                var deserialized = JsonSerializer.Deserialize<JsonValue>(ref reader, options);
+                Console.WriteLine("Deserialized JsonValue type: " + deserialized?.GetType());
+                Console.WriteLine("SUCCESS: No exception");
+            }
+            catch (Exception ex)
+            {
+                Console.WriteLine("ERROR: " + ex);
+            }
+            
+            // Test the actual issue described in PR
+            TestSpecificIssue();
+        }
+        
+        static void TestSpecificIssue()
+        {
+            Console.WriteLine("\n=== Testing specific issue ===");
+            var original = JsonValue.Create(1);
+            Console.WriteLine("Original: " + original.GetType());
+            
+            // This simulates what might be happening in Orleans serialization
+            var jsonString = JsonSerializer.Serialize(original);
+            Console.WriteLine("JSON: " + jsonString);
+            
+            // Try to deserialize to JsonNode (which is what the grain method expects)
+            try
+            {
+                var deserialized = JsonSerializer.Deserialize<JsonNode>(jsonString);
+                Console.WriteLine("Deserialized: " + deserialized?.GetType());
+                
+                // Try to cast to JsonValue (this is likely where the issue occurs)
+                var asJsonValue = deserialized as JsonValue;
+                Console.WriteLine("As JsonValue: " + (asJsonValue != null ? asJsonValue.GetType().ToString() : "null"));
+                
+                // Try explicit cast (this might throw)
+                try
+                {
+                    var explicitCast = (JsonValue)deserialized!;
+                    Console.WriteLine("Explicit cast successful: " + explicitCast.GetType());
+                }
+                catch (InvalidCastException icex)
+                {
+                    Console.WriteLine("INVALID CAST: " + icex.Message);
+                }
+            }
+            catch (Exception ex)
+            {
+                Console.WriteLine("ERROR: " + ex);
+            }
+        }
+    }
+}

+using System;
+using System.Text.Json.Nodes;
+using System.Text.Json;
+
+namespace TestJsonValueFix
+{
+    class Program
+    {
+        static void Main(string[] args)
+        {
+            Console.WriteLine("=== Testing JsonValue fix approach ===\n");
+            
+            // Test the proposed fix
+            TestProposedFix();
+        }
+        
+        static void TestProposedFix()
+        {
+            var original = JsonValue.Create(1);
+            var originalType = original.GetType();
+            Console.WriteLine($"Original: {originalType}");
+            
+            var json = JsonSerializer.Serialize(original);
+            Console.WriteLine($"JSON: {json}");
+            
+            // The fix: handle JsonValue types specially
+            JsonNode result = HandleJsonValueDeserialization(json, originalType);
+            Console.WriteLine($"Result: {result?.GetType()}");
+            Console.WriteLine($"Match: {result?.GetType() == originalType}");
+            
+            // Test edge cases
+            TestEdgeCases();
+        }
+        
+        static JsonNode HandleJsonValueDeserialization(string json, Type targetType)
+        {
+            // If target type is or inherits from JsonValue
+            if (typeof(JsonValue).IsAssignableFrom(targetType))
+            {
+                // First, deserialize to JsonNode
+                var asNode = JsonSerializer.Deserialize<JsonNode>(json);
+                
+                if (asNode is JsonValue jsonValue)
+                {
+                    // Get the underlying value
+                    var underlyingValue = jsonValue.GetValue<object>();
+                    
+                    if (underlyingValue is JsonElement jsonElement)
+                    {
+                        // Extract the actual value from JsonElement
+                        var actualValue = ExtractValueFromJsonElement(jsonElement);
+                        
+                        // Create appropriate JsonValue
+                        var recreated = JsonValue.Create(actualValue);
+                        
+                        // If the target type is a specific JsonValuePrimitive<T>, 
+                        // we need to ensure compatibility
+                        if (targetType.IsGenericType && 
+                            targetType.GetGenericTypeDefinition() == typeof(JsonValuePrimitive<>))
+                        {
+                            var targetGenericArg = targetType.GetGenericArguments()[0];
+                            var resultGenericArg = recreated?.GetType().GetGenericArguments()[0];
+                            
+                            // If the generic arguments don't match, we may need to convert
+                            if (targetGenericArg != resultGenericArg)
+                            {
+                                // Convert the value to the target type if possible
+                                var convertedValue = Convert.ChangeType(actualValue, targetGenericArg);
+                                recreated = JsonValue.Create(convertedValue);
+                            }
+                        }
+                        
+                        return recreated;
+                    }
+                }
+                
+                return asNode;
+            }
+            
+            // Fall back to normal deserialization
+            return (JsonNode)JsonSerializer.Deserialize(json, targetType);
+        }
+        
+        static object? ExtractValueFromJsonElement(JsonElement element)
+        {
+            return element.ValueKind switch
+            {
+                JsonValueKind.Number when element.TryGetInt32(out int intValue) => intValue,
+                JsonValueKind.Number when element.TryGetInt64(out long longValue) => longValue,
+                JsonValueKind.Number when element.TryGetDouble(out double doubleValue) => doubleValue,
+                JsonValueKind.True => true,
+                JsonValueKind.False => false,
+                JsonValueKind.String => element.GetString(),
+                JsonValueKind.Null => null,
+                _ => element // fallback
+            };
+        }
+        
+        static void TestEdgeCases()
+        {
+            Console.WriteLine("\n=== Testing edge cases ===");
+            
+            // Test different JsonValue types
+            TestWithValue(JsonValue.Create(true));
+            TestWithValue(JsonValue.Create("hello"));
+            TestWithValue(JsonValue.Create(3.14));
+            TestWithValue(JsonValue.Create((string?)null));
+            
+            // Test JsonObject and JsonArray (should not be affected)
+            TestWithValue(new JsonObject { ["key"] = "value" });
+            TestWithValue(new JsonArray { 1, 2, 3 });
+        }
+        
+        static void TestWithValue(JsonNode value)
+        {
+            var originalType = value.GetType();
+            var json = JsonSerializer.Serialize(value);
+            
+            var result = HandleJsonValueDeserialization(json, originalType);
+            Console.WriteLine($"{originalType.Name} -> {result?.GetType().Name}: Match = {result?.GetType() == originalType}");
+        }
+    }
+}

+using System;
+using System.Text.Json.Nodes;
+using System.Text.Json;
+
+namespace TestJsonValueFix
+{
+    class Program
+    {
+        static void Main(string[] args)
+        {
+            Console.WriteLine("=== Testing JsonValue fix approach ===\n");
+            
+            // Test the proposed fix
+            TestProposedFix();
+        }
+        
+        static void TestProposedFix()
+        {
+            var original = JsonValue.Create(1);
+            var originalType = original.GetType();
+            Console.WriteLine($"Original: {originalType}");
+            
+            var json = JsonSerializer.Serialize(original);
+            Console.WriteLine($"JSON: {json}");
+            
+            // The fix: handle JsonValue types specially
+            JsonNode? result = HandleJsonValueDeserialization(json, originalType);
+            Console.WriteLine($"Result: {result?.GetType()}");
+            Console.WriteLine($"Match: {result?.GetType() == originalType}");
+            
+            if (result is JsonValue resultValue)
+            {
+                Console.WriteLine($"Extracted value: {resultValue.GetValue<object>()}");
+            }
+            
+            // Test edge cases
+            TestEdgeCases();
+        }
+        
+        static JsonNode? HandleJsonValueDeserialization(string json, Type targetType)
+        {
+            // If target type is or inherits from JsonValue
+            if (typeof(JsonValue).IsAssignableFrom(targetType))
+            {
+                // First, deserialize to JsonNode
+                var asNode = JsonSerializer.Deserialize<JsonNode>(json);
+                
+                if (asNode is JsonValue jsonValue)
+                {
+                    // Get the underlying value
+                    var underlyingValue = jsonValue.GetValue<object>();
+                    
+                    if (underlyingValue is JsonElement jsonElement)
+                    {
+                        // Extract the actual value from JsonElement
+                        var actualValue = ExtractValueFromJsonElement(jsonElement);
+                        
+                        if (actualValue != null)
+                        {
+                            // Create appropriate JsonValue
+                            var recreated = JsonValue.Create(actualValue);
+                            return recreated;
+                        }
+                    }
+                }
+                
+                return asNode;
+            }
+            
+            // Fall back to normal deserialization
+            try
+            {
+                return (JsonNode?)JsonSerializer.Deserialize(json, targetType);
+            }
+            catch (InvalidCastException)
+            {
+                // If direct deserialization fails, try the JsonNode approach
+                var asNode = JsonSerializer.Deserialize<JsonNode>(json);
+                return asNode;
+            }
+        }
+        
+        static object? ExtractValueFromJsonElement(JsonElement element)
+        {
+            return element.ValueKind switch
+            {
+                JsonValueKind.Number when element.TryGetInt32(out int intValue) => intValue,
+                JsonValueKind.Number when element.TryGetInt64(out long longValue) => longValue,
+                JsonValueKind.Number when element.TryGetDouble(out double doubleValue) => doubleValue,
+                JsonValueKind.True => true,
+                JsonValueKind.False => false,
+                JsonValueKind.String => element.GetString(),
+                JsonValueKind.Null => null,
+                _ => element // fallback
+            };
+        }
+        
+        static void TestEdgeCases()
+        {
+            Console.WriteLine("\n=== Testing edge cases ===");
+            
+            // Test different JsonValue types
+            TestWithValue(JsonValue.Create(true));
+            TestWithValue(JsonValue.Create("hello"));
+            TestWithValue(JsonValue.Create(3.14));
+            
+            // Test JsonObject and JsonArray (should not be affected)
+            TestWithValue(new JsonObject { ["key"] = "value" });
+            TestWithValue(new JsonArray { 1, 2, 3 });
+        }
+        
+        static void TestWithValue(JsonNode value)
+        {
+            var originalType = value.GetType();
+            var json = JsonSerializer.Serialize(value);
+            
+            var result = HandleJsonValueDeserialization(json, originalType);
+            Console.WriteLine($"{originalType.Name} -> {result?.GetType().Name}: Match = {result?.GetType() == originalType}");
+        }
+    }
+}

+using System;
+using System.Text.Json.Nodes;
+using System.Reflection;
+using System.Text.Json;
+
+namespace TestJsonValueIssue
+{
+    class Program
+    {
+        static void Main(string[] args)
+        {
+            Console.WriteLine("=== Detailed analysis of JsonValue types ===\n");
+            
+            // Test JsonValue.Create with different types
+            TestJsonValueType(JsonValue.Create(1), "JsonValue.Create(1)");
+            TestJsonValueType(JsonValue.Create(true), "JsonValue.Create(true)");
+            TestJsonValueType(JsonValue.Create("hello"), "JsonValue.Create(\"hello\")");
+            
+            // Test serialization/deserialization issue
+            Console.WriteLine("\n=== Testing serialization issue ===");
+            TestSerializationIssue();
+        }
+        
+        static void TestJsonValueType(JsonValue value, string description)
+        {
+            Console.WriteLine($"{description}:");
+            Console.WriteLine($"  Type: {value.GetType().FullName}");
+            Console.WriteLine($"  IsGenericType: {value.GetType().IsGenericType}");
+            
+            if (value.GetType().IsGenericType)
+            {
+                var genericArgs = value.GetType().GetGenericArguments();
+                Console.WriteLine($"  Generic arguments: {string.Join<Type>(", ", genericArgs)}");
+                Console.WriteLine($"  Generic definition: {value.GetType().GetGenericTypeDefinition()}");
+            }
+            
+            // Check base types
+            Console.WriteLine($"  Is JsonValue: {value is JsonValue}");
+            Console.WriteLine($"  Is JsonNode: {value is JsonNode}");
+            Console.WriteLine();
+        }
+        
+        static void TestSerializationIssue()
+        {
+            // Create the problematic JsonValue
+            var original = JsonValue.Create(1);
+            Console.WriteLine($"Original: {original.GetType().FullName}");
+            
+            // Serialize and deserialize like Orleans does
+            var options = new JsonSerializerOptions();
+            var json = JsonSerializer.Serialize(original, options);
+            Console.WriteLine($"Serialized JSON: {json}");
+            
+            // Key issue: Deserializing to JsonNode returns JsonValuePrimitive<JsonElement>
+            // instead of preserving the original JsonValuePrimitive<int>
+            var deserializedAsNode = JsonSerializer.Deserialize<JsonNode>(json, options);
+            Console.WriteLine($"Deserialized as JsonNode: {deserializedAsNode?.GetType().FullName}");
+            
+            // Try to get back as JsonValue
+            var deserializedAsValue = JsonSerializer.Deserialize<JsonValue>(json, options);
+            Console.WriteLine($"Deserialized as JsonValue: {deserializedAsValue?.GetType().FullName}");
+            
+            // The issue: Orleans likely stores the TYPE information as typeof(JsonValue) or typeof(JsonNode)
+            // but when deserializing, System.Text.Json creates a JsonValuePrimitive<JsonElement> instead
+            // of preserving the original JsonValuePrimitive<int>
+            
+            Console.WriteLine("\n=== Testing cast scenario from PR ===");
+            
+            // Simulate what happens in Orleans:
+            // 1. Grain method expects JsonNode parameter
+            // 2. Client sends JsonValue.Create(1) which is JsonValuePrimitive<int>
+            // 3. After serialization/deserialization, it becomes JsonValuePrimitive<JsonElement>
+            // 4. When Orleans tries to pass it to the grain method, there might be a type mismatch
+            
+            // The cast that might fail
+            try
+            {
+                // This simulates what Orleans might be doing internally
+                var asJsonNode = (JsonNode)original;
+                Console.WriteLine($"Original as JsonNode: {asJsonNode.GetType().FullName}");
+                
+                // After round-trip serialization
+                var roundTripped = JsonSerializer.Deserialize<JsonNode>(JsonSerializer.Serialize(original, options), options);
+                Console.WriteLine($"Round-tripped as JsonNode: {roundTripped?.GetType().FullName}");
+                
+                // This cast should work but might reveal the underlying issue
+                var asOriginalType = roundTripped as JsonValue;
+                Console.WriteLine($"Round-tripped as JsonValue: {asOriginalType?.GetType().FullName ?? "null"}");
+                
+                // The problematic scenario:
+                // If Orleans stores the type as the original JsonValuePrimitive<int>
+                // but the actual deserialized object is JsonValuePrimitive<JsonElement>
+                // this causes InvalidCastException
+                
+                Console.WriteLine("\n=== Testing the actual InvalidCastException ===");
+                
+                // Get the assembly to access internal types
+                var jsonNodeAssembly = typeof(JsonNode).Assembly;
+                
+                // Try to find the JsonValueOfElement type (mentioned in the error)
+                var jsonValueOfElementType = jsonNodeAssembly.GetType("System.Text.Json.Nodes.JsonValueOfElement");
+                Console.WriteLine($"JsonValueOfElement type found: {jsonValueOfElementType != null}");
+                
+                if (jsonValueOfElementType != null)
+                {
+                    // Check if our deserialized value is of this type
+                    Console.WriteLine($"Deserialized is JsonValueOfElement: {jsonValueOfElementType.IsInstanceOfType(deserializedAsValue)}");
+                }
+                
+                // Check if we can reproduce the exact error
+                TestExactErrorScenario();
+                
+            }
+            catch (Exception ex)
+            {
+                Console.WriteLine($"ERROR: {ex}");
+            }
+        }
+        
+        static void TestExactErrorScenario()
+        {
+            Console.WriteLine("\n=== Attempting to reproduce exact error ===");
+            
+            // Based on the PR description, the error is:
+            // "Unable to cast object of type 'System.Text.Json.Nodes.JsonValueOfElement' 
+            // to type 'System.Text.Json.Nodes.JsonValuePrimitive`1[System.Int32]'"
+            
+            // This suggests that somewhere in Orleans, there's code that tries to cast
+            // from JsonValueOfElement to JsonValuePrimitive<int>
+            
+            var original = JsonValue.Create(1);
+            var json = JsonSerializer.Serialize(original);
+            var deserialized = JsonSerializer.Deserialize<JsonValue>(json);
+            
+            Console.WriteLine($"Original type: {original.GetType()}");
+            Console.WriteLine($"Deserialized type: {deserialized?.GetType()}");
+            
+            // Try to force the problematic cast
+            try
+            {
+                // This might be what's happening internally
+                // Orleans might have stored the expected type as JsonValuePrimitive<int>
+                // but the actual object is a different JsonValue subtype
+                
+                // Get MethodInfo for a hypothetical cast operation
+                var originalType = original.GetType();
+                var deserializedType = deserialized?.GetType();
+                
+                if (originalType != deserializedType)
+                {
+                    Console.WriteLine($"TYPE MISMATCH! Original: {originalType}, Deserialized: {deserializedType}");
+                    
+                    // Try explicit cast which should fail
+                    if (deserialized != null)
+                    {
+                        var casted = Convert.ChangeType(deserialized, originalType);
+                        Console.WriteLine($"Cast succeeded: {casted.GetType()}");
+                    }
+                }
+            }
+            catch (InvalidCastException ex)
+            {
+                Console.WriteLine($"INVALID CAST (expected): {ex.Message}");
+                
+                // Check if it matches the PR error
+                if (ex.Message.Contains("JsonValueOfElement") && ex.Message.Contains("JsonValuePrimitive"))
+                {
+                    Console.WriteLine("*** MATCHES PR ERROR DESCRIPTION ***");
+                }
+            }
+            catch (Exception ex)
+            {
+                Console.WriteLine($"Other error: {ex.Message}");
+            }
+        }
+    }
+}

+using System;
+using System.Text.Json.Nodes;
+using System.Text.Json;
+using System.IO;
+using System.Buffers;
+
+namespace TestOrleansSerialization
+{
+    class Program
+    {
+        static void Main(string[] args)
+        {
+            TestIssue();
+        }
+        
+        static void TestIssue()
+        {
+            Console.WriteLine("=== Testing Orleans serialization issue ===");
+            
+            // Create JsonValue with int (this is what fails)
+            var originalValue = JsonValue.Create(1);
+            Console.WriteLine($"Original Value Type: {originalValue.GetType()}");
+            
+            // This is equivalent to what JsonCodec does
+            var options = new JsonSerializerOptions();
+            
+            // Step 1: Serialize the JsonValue
+            byte[] jsonBytes;
+            using (var memoryStream = new MemoryStream())
+            {
+                using (var jsonWriter = new Utf8JsonWriter(memoryStream))
+                {
+                    JsonSerializer.Serialize(jsonWriter, originalValue, options);
+                }
+                jsonBytes = memoryStream.ToArray();
+            }
+            Console.WriteLine($"Serialized JSON: {System.Text.Encoding.UTF8.GetString(jsonBytes)}");
+            
+            // Step 2: Try to deserialize back to JsonNode (which Orleans might be doing)
+            var reader = new Utf8JsonReader(jsonBytes);
+            var deserialized = JsonSerializer.Deserialize<JsonNode>(ref reader, options);
+            Console.WriteLine($"Deserialized Type: {deserialized?.GetType()}");
+            
+            // The issue: original was JsonValuePrimitive<int> but deserialized is JsonValuePrimitive<JsonElement>
+            // This causes InvalidCastException when trying to cast between them
+            
+            // Test the problematic cast
+            try
+            {
+                var castedValue = (JsonValue)deserialized!;
+                Console.WriteLine("Direct cast succeeded");
+            }
+            catch (InvalidCastException ex)
+            {
+                Console.WriteLine($"INVALID CAST: {ex.Message}");
+                Console.WriteLine($"Exception Type: {ex.GetType()}");
+                
+                // Check if this matches the error from the PR description
+                if (ex.Message.Contains("JsonValueOfElement") && ex.Message.Contains("JsonValuePrimitive"))
+                {
+                    Console.WriteLine("THIS IS THE EXACT ERROR FROM THE PR!");
+                }
+            }
+            
+            Console.WriteLine("\n=== Testing JsonValue.Create(true) ===");
+            TestWithBool();
+        }
+        
+        static void TestWithBool()
+        {
+            var originalValue = JsonValue.Create(true);
+            Console.WriteLine($"Original Value Type: {originalValue.GetType()}");
+            
+            var options = new JsonSerializerOptions();
+            
+            // Step 1: Serialize the JsonValue
+            byte[] jsonBytes;
+            using (var memoryStream = new MemoryStream())
+            {
+                using (var jsonWriter = new Utf8JsonWriter(memoryStream))
+                {
+                    JsonSerializer.Serialize(jsonWriter, originalValue, options);
+                }
+                jsonBytes = memoryStream.ToArray();
+            }
+            
+            // Step 2: Try to deserialize back to JsonNode
+            var reader = new Utf8JsonReader(jsonBytes);
+            var deserialized = JsonSerializer.Deserialize<JsonNode>(ref reader, options);
+            Console.WriteLine($"Deserialized Type: {deserialized?.GetType()}");
+            
+            // Test cast
+            try
+            {
+                var castedValue = (JsonValue)deserialized!;
+                Console.WriteLine("Direct cast succeeded");
+            }
+            catch (InvalidCastException ex)
+            {
+                Console.WriteLine($"INVALID CAST: {ex.Message}");
+            }
+        }
+    }
+}

+using System;
+using System.Text.Json.Nodes;
+using Orleans.Serialization.SystemTextJson;
+using Microsoft.Extensions.DependencyInjection;
+
+namespace TestSimpleFix
+{
+    class Program
+    {
+        static void Main(string[] args)
+        {
+            Console.WriteLine("=== Testing JsonValue serialization fix ===\n");
+            
+            // Create service provider with JSON serialization
+            var services = new ServiceCollection();
+            services.AddSerializer()
+                .AddJsonSerializer(isSupportedType: type => typeof(JsonNode).IsAssignableFrom(type));
+            
+            var serviceProvider = services.BuildServiceProvider();
+            var serializer = serviceProvider.GetRequiredService<Serializer>();
+            
+            // Test case: JsonValue created with int (the problematic case from the PR)
+            var jsonValue = JsonValue.Create(1);
+            Console.WriteLine("Original type: " + jsonValue.GetType());
+            Console.WriteLine("Value: " + jsonValue);
+            
+            try
+            {
+                // Serialize and deserialize
+                var serialized = serializer.SerializeToArray(jsonValue);
+                var deserialized = serializer.Deserialize(serialized);
+                
+                Console.WriteLine("Deserialized type: " + deserialized?.GetType());
+                Console.WriteLine("Deserialized value: " + deserialized);
+                
+                // Test if we can cast to JsonValue (this was failing before)
+                if (deserialized is JsonValue deserializedValue)
+                {
+                    Console.WriteLine("Cast to JsonValue successful");
+                    Console.WriteLine("Extracted value: " + deserializedValue.GetValue<object>());
+                }
+                
+                Console.WriteLine("SUCCESS: No exception occurred");
+            }
+            catch (InvalidCastException ex)
+            {
+                Console.WriteLine("INVALID CAST ERROR: " + ex.Message);
+                Console.WriteLine("This indicates the fix did not work properly");
+            }
+            catch (Exception ex)
+            {
+                Console.WriteLine("OTHER ERROR: " + ex.ToString());
+            }
+        }
+    }
+}

diff --git a/add_methods.txt b/add_methods.txt
new file mode 100644
index 000000000..a29e76b0d
--- /dev/null
+++ b/add_methods.txt
@@ -0,0 +1,40 @@
+
+        private object? DeserializeJsonValue(ref Utf8JsonReader jsonReader, Type targetType)
+        {
+            // First deserialize to JsonNode to avoid JsonValuePrimitive type mismatches
+            var jsonNode = JsonSerializer.Deserialize<JsonNode>(ref jsonReader, _options.SerializerOptions);
+            
+            if (jsonNode is JsonValue jsonValue)
+            {
+                // Get the underlying value
+                var underlyingValue = jsonValue.GetValue<object>();
+                
+                // If the underlying value is JsonElement, extract the actual value
+                if (underlyingValue is JsonElement jsonElement)
+                {
+                    var actualValue = ExtractValueFromJsonElement(jsonElement);
+                    if (actualValue != null)
+                    {
+                        // Create a new JsonValue with the actual value
+                        return JsonValue.Create(actualValue);
+                    }
+                }
+            }
+            
+            return jsonNode;
+        }
+        
+        private static object? ExtractValueFromJsonElement(JsonElement element)
+        {
+            return element.ValueKind switch
+            {
+                JsonValueKind.Number when element.TryGetInt32(out int intValue) => intValue,
+                JsonValueKind.Number when element.TryGetInt64(out long longValue) => longValue,
+                JsonValueKind.Number when element.TryGetDouble(out double doubleValue) => doubleValue,
+                JsonValueKind.True => true,
+                JsonValueKind.False => false,
+                JsonValueKind.String => element.GetString(),
+                JsonValueKind.Null => null,
+                _ => element // fallback
+            };
+        }
diff --git a/analyze_json_codec.cs b/analyze_json_codec.cs
new file mode 100644
index 000000000..65d07ef27
--- /dev/null
+++ b/analyze_json_codec.cs
@@ -0,0 +1,114 @@
+using System;
+using System.Text.Json.Nodes;
+using System.Text.Json;
+
+namespace AnalyzeJsonCodec
+{
+    class Program
+    {
+        static void Main(string[] args)
+        {
+            // The issue is in how Orleans JsonCodec handles JsonValue serialization
+            // When it serializes JsonValue.Create(1):
+            // - It stores the type as JsonValuePrimitive<int>
+            // - It serializes the value as JSON: 1
+            
+            // When deserializing:
+            // - It reads the stored type: JsonValuePrimitive<int>  
+            // - It tries to deserialize JSON: 1 to that type
+            // - But System.Text.Json.Deserialize with JsonValuePrimitive<int> doesn't work correctly
+            
+            Console.WriteLine("=== Analyzing the JsonCodec issue ===\n");
+            
+            // Test what happens when we try to deserialize directly to JsonValuePrimitive<int>
+            TestDirectDeserialization();
+            
+            // Test the workaround that Orleans should use
+            TestWorkaround();
+        }
+        
+        static void TestDirectDeserialization()
+        {
+            Console.WriteLine("=== Testing direct deserialization to JsonValuePrimitive<int> ===");
+            
+            var original = JsonValue.Create(1);
+            Console.WriteLine($"Original: {original.GetType()}");
+            
+            var json = JsonSerializer.Serialize(original);
+            Console.WriteLine($"JSON: {json}");
+            
+            // This is what Orleans JsonCodec tries to do
+            try
+            {
+                // Try to deserialize directly to the original type
+                var options = new JsonSerializerOptions();
+                var deserialized = JsonSerializer.Deserialize(json, original.GetType(), options);
+                Console.WriteLine($"Direct deserialization result: {deserialized?.GetType() ?? Type.GetType("null")}");
+                
+                if (deserialized != null)
+                {
+                    Console.WriteLine($"Value: {deserialized}");
+                }
+            }
+            catch (Exception ex)
+            {
+                Console.WriteLine($"DIRECT DESERIALIZATION FAILED: {ex.Message}");
+                Console.WriteLine($"Exception type: {ex.GetType()}");
+            }
+        }
+        
+        static void TestWorkaround()
+        {
+            Console.WriteLine("\n=== Testing workaround ===");
+            
+            var original = JsonValue.Create(1);
+            var json = JsonSerializer.Serialize(original);
+            
+            // The correct approach: deserialize to JsonNode first, then handle conversion
+            var deserializedNode = JsonSerializer.Deserialize<JsonNode>(json);
+            Console.WriteLine($"Deserialized as JsonNode: {deserializedNode?.GetType()}");
+            
+            // Now we need to convert it back to the original type
+            // The issue is that JsonValuePrimitive<JsonElement> != JsonValuePrimitive<int>
+            // but they both implement JsonValue and have the same underlying value
+            
+            if (deserializedNode is JsonValue jsonValue)
+            {
+                Console.WriteLine($"It's a JsonValue: {jsonValue.GetType()}");
+                
+                // Get the underlying value
+                var underlyingValue = jsonValue.GetValue<object>();
+                Console.WriteLine($"Underlying value: {underlyingValue} (type: {underlyingValue.GetType()})");
+                
+                // We can recreate the original JsonValue by using JsonValue.Create with the underlying value
+                var recreated = JsonValue.Create(underlyingValue);
+                Console.WriteLine($"Recreated: {recreated.GetType()}");
+                
+                // But this still won't be JsonValuePrimitive<int> if underlyingValue is JsonElement
+                // We need to extract the actual value from JsonElement
+                
+                if (underlyingValue is JsonElement jsonElement)
+                {
+                    Console.WriteLine("Underlying value is JsonElement, extracting actual value...");
+                    
+                    object actualValue = jsonElement.ValueKind switch
+                    {
+                        JsonValueKind.Number when jsonElement.TryGetInt32(out int intValue) => intValue,
+                        JsonValueKind.Number when jsonElement.TryGetInt64(out long longValue) => longValue,
+                        JsonValueKind.Number when jsonElement.TryGetDouble(out double doubleValue) => doubleValue,
+                        JsonValueKind.True => true,
+                        JsonValueKind.False => false,
+                        JsonValueKind.String => jsonElement.GetString(),
+                        JsonValueKind.Null => null,
+                        _ => jsonElement // fallback
+                    };
+                    
+                    Console.WriteLine($"Extracted actual value: {actualValue} (type: {actualValue?.GetType()})");
+                    
+                    var properlyRecreated = JsonValue.Create(actualValue);
+                    Console.WriteLine($"Properly recreated: {properlyRecreated?.GetType()}");
+                }
+            }
+        }
+    }
+}

+import sys
+
+# Read the original file
+with open('./src/Orleans.Serialization.SystemTextJson/JsonCodec.cs', 'r') as f:
+    lines = f.readlines()
+
+# Find the line to replace and the method end
+replace_line = None
+record_object_line = None
+
+for i, line in enumerate(lines):
+    if 'result = JsonSerializer.Deserialize(ref jsonReader, type, _options.SerializerOptions);' in line:
+        replace_line = i
+    if 'ReferenceCodec.RecordObject(reader.Session, result, placeholderReferenceId);' in line and i > (replace_line or 0):
+        record_object_line = i
+        break
+
+if replace_line is None or record_object_line is None:
+    print("Could not find the target lines")
+    sys.exit(1)
+
+# Create the new content
+new_lines = []
+new_lines.extend(lines[:replace_line])
+
+# Replace the deserialization line
+new_lines.append('                        // Special handling for JsonValue types to avoid InvalidCastException\n')
+new_lines.append('                        if (typeof(JsonValue).IsAssignableFrom(type))\n')
+new_lines.append('                        {\n')
+new_lines.append('                            result = DeserializeJsonValue(ref jsonReader, type);\n')
+new_lines.append('                        }\n')
+new_lines.append('                        else\n')
+new_lines.append('                        {\n')
+new_lines.append('                            result = JsonSerializer.Deserialize(ref jsonReader, type, _options.SerializerOptions);\n')
+new_lines.append('                        }\n')
+
+# Add remaining lines until RecordObject
+new_lines.extend(lines[replace_line + 1:record_object_line + 1])
+
+# Add helper methods after RecordObject
+new_lines.append('\n')
+new_lines.append('        private object? DeserializeJsonValue(ref Utf8JsonReader jsonReader, Type targetType)\n')
+new_lines.append('        {\n')
+new_lines.append('            // First deserialize to JsonNode to avoid JsonValuePrimitive type mismatches\n')
+new_lines.append('            var jsonNode = JsonSerializer.Deserialize<JsonNode>(ref jsonReader, _options.SerializerOptions);\n')
+new_lines.append('            \n')
+new_lines.append('            if (jsonNode is JsonValue jsonValue)\n')
+new_lines.append('            {\n')
+new_lines.append('                // Get the underlying value\n')
+new_lines.append('                var underlyingValue = jsonValue.GetValue<object>();\n')
+new_lines.append('                \n')
+new_lines.append('                // If the underlying value is JsonElement, extract the actual value\n')
+new_lines.append('                if (underlyingValue is JsonElement jsonElement)\n')
+new_lines.append('                {\n')
+new_lines.append('                    var actualValue = ExtractValueFromJsonElement(jsonElement);\n')
+new_lines.append('                    if (actualValue != null)\n')
+new_lines.append('                    {\n')
+new_lines.append('                        // Create a new JsonValue with the actual value\n')
+new_lines.append('                        return JsonValue.Create(actualValue);\n')
+new_lines.append('                    }\n')
+new_lines.append('                }\n')
+new_lines.append('            }\n')
+new_lines.append('            \n')
+new_lines.append('            return jsonNode;\n')
+new_lines.append('        }\n')
+new_lines.append('        \n')
+new_lines.append('        private static object? ExtractValueFromJsonElement(JsonElement element)\n')
+new_lines.append('        {\n')
+new_lines.append('            return element.ValueKind switch\n')
+new_lines.append('            {\n')
+new_lines.append('                JsonValueKind.Number when element.TryGetInt32(out int intValue) => intValue,\n')
+new_lines.append('                JsonValueKind.Number when element.TryGetInt64(out long longValue) => longValue,\n')
+new_lines.append('                JsonValueKind.Number when element.TryGetDouble(out double doubleValue) => doubleValue,\n')
+new_lines.append('                JsonValueKind.True => true,\n')
+new_lines.append('                JsonValueKind.False => false,\n')
+new_lines.append('                JsonValueKind.String => element.GetString(),\n')
+new_lines.append('                JsonValueKind.Null => null,\n')
+new_lines.append('                _ => element // fallback\n')
+new_lines.append('            };\n')
+new_lines.append('        }\n')
+new_lines.append('\n')
+
+# Add the rest of the file
+new_lines.extend(lines[record_object_line + 1:])
+
+# Write the fixed file
+with open('./src/Orleans.Serialization.SystemTextJson/JsonCodec.cs', 'w') as f:
+    f.writelines(new_lines)
+
+print("Fix applied successfully")
diff --git a/fix_analysis.md b/fix_analysis.md
new file mode 100644
index 000000000..4374432ce
--- /dev/null
+++ b/fix_analysis.md
@@ -0,0 +1,33 @@
+# Analysis of JsonCodec Issue
+
+## Problem
+When Orleans serializes JsonValue.Create(1):
+- Original type: JsonValuePrimitive<int>
+- Serialized JSON: "1"
+- Stored type info: JsonValuePrimitive<int>
+
+When Orleans deserializes:
+- Tries to deserialize "1" to JsonValuePrimitive<int>
+- System.Text.Json creates JsonValuePrimitive<JsonElement> instead
+- InvalidCastException when casting between these types
+
+## Root Cause
+System.Text.Json's JsonSerializer.Deserialize method cannot properly reconstruct 
+JsonValuePrimitive<T> with the original T parameter when T is a primitive type.
+Instead, it creates JsonValuePrimitive<JsonElement>.
+
+## Solution Options
+1. **Fix in ReadValue method**: When deserializing JsonValue types:
+   - First deserialize to JsonNode
+   - Then convert to the expected JsonValue type
+   - Extract actual value from JsonElement if needed
+
+2. **Special handling for JsonValue types**: Detect when the target type is JsonValue
+   and use JsonNode as intermediate type.
+
+## Implementation Plan
+1. Modify the ReadValue method to detect JsonValue types
+2. Add special handling for JsonValues:
+   - Deserialize to JsonNode first
+   - Convert to the target JsonValue type
+   - Handle JsonElement extraction if needed

+import re
+
+# Read the file
+with open('./src/Orleans.Serialization.SystemTextJson/JsonCodec.cs', 'r') as f:
+    content = f.read()
+
+# Find the section we need to replace
+old_section = '''                    try
+                    {
+                        reader.ReadBytes(ref tempBuffer, (int)length);
+                        var sequence = tempBuffer.AsReadOnlySequence();
+                        var jsonReader = new Utf8JsonReader(sequence, _options.ReaderOptions);
+                        result = JsonSerializer.Deserialize(ref jsonReader, type, _options.SerializerOptions);
+                    }
+                    finally
+                    {
+                        tempBuffer.Dispose();
+                    }
+
+                    break;'''
+
+new_section = '''                    try
+                    {
+                        reader.ReadBytes(ref tempBuffer, (int)length);
+                        var sequence = tempBuffer.AsReadOnlySequence();
+                        var jsonReader = new Utf8JsonReader(sequence, _options.ReaderOptions);
+                        
+                        // Special handling for JsonValue types to avoid InvalidCastException
+                        if (typeof(JsonValue).IsAssignableFrom(type))
+                        {
+                            result = DeserializeJsonValue(ref jsonReader, type);
+                        }
+                        else
+                        {
+                            result = JsonSerializer.Deserialize(ref jsonReader, type, _options.SerializerOptions);
+                        }
+                    }
+                    finally
+                    {
+                        tempBuffer.Dispose();
+                    }
+
+                    break;'''
+
+# Replace the section
+content = content.replace(old_section, new_section)
+
+# Write back to file
+with open('./src/Orleans.Serialization.SystemTextJson/JsonCodec.cs', 'w') as f:
+    f.write(content)
+
+print('Replacement successful')

+# Simple fix approach - edit the file directly with proper context
+
+# Read the original file
+with open('./src/Orleans.Serialization.SystemTextJson/JsonCodec.cs', 'r') as f:
+    lines = f.readlines()
+
+# Find the line we need to modify (around line 138)
+for i, line in enumerate(lines):
+    if "result = JsonSerializer.Deserialize(ref jsonReader, type, _options.SerializerOptions);" in line:
+        # Replace this line with our fix
+        lines[i] = "                        \"\"\"\"\"Special handling for JsonValue types to avoid InvalidCastException\\\\n                        if (typeof(JsonValue).IsAssignableFrom(type))\\\\n                        {\\\\n                            result = JsonSerializer.Deserialize<JsonNode>(ref jsonReader, _options.SerializerOptions);\\\\n                            // Additional JsonValue handling will be applied later\\\\n                        }\\\\n                        else\\\\n                        {\\\\n                            result = JsonSerializer.Deserialize(ref jsonReader, type, _options.SerializerOptions);\\\\n                        }\\\\n"
+        break
+
+# Write the partially fixed file back
+with open('./src/Orleans.Serialization.SystemTextJson/JsonCodec.cs', 'w') as f:
+    f.writelines(lines)
+
+print("Partial fix applied")

+using System;
+using System.Text.Json.Nodes;
+using Orleans.Serialization;
+using Microsoft.Extensions.DependencyInjection;
+
+namespace ReproduceIssue
+{
+    class Program
+    {
+        static void Main(string[] args)
+        {
+            // Create service provider with JSON serialization
+            var services = new ServiceCollection();
+            services.AddSerializer(serializerBuilder =>
+            {
+                serializerBuilder.AddJsonSerializer();
+            });
+            
+            var serviceProvider = services.BuildServiceProvider();
+            var serializer = serviceProvider.GetRequiredService<Serializer>();
+            
+            // Test case: JsonValue created with int
+            var jsonValue = JsonValue.Create(1);
+            Console.WriteLine("Original type: " + jsonValue.GetType());
+            Console.WriteLine("Value: " + jsonValue);
+            
+            try
+            {
+                // Serialize and deserialize
+                var serialized = serializer.Serialize(jsonValue);
+                var deserialized = serializer.Deserialize(serialized);
+                
+                Console.WriteLine("Deserialized type: " + deserialized.GetType());
+                Console.WriteLine("Deserialized value: " + deserialized);
+                Console.WriteLine("SUCCESS: No exception occurred");
+            }
+            catch (Exception ex)
+            {
+                Console.WriteLine("ERROR: " + ex.ToString());
+            }
+        }
+    }
+}

diff --git a/src/Orleans.Serialization.SystemTextJson/JsonCodec.cs.backup b/src/Orleans.Serialization.SystemTextJson/JsonCodec.cs.backup
new file mode 100644
index 000000000..ab8ace8b2

+++ b/src/Orleans.Serialization.SystemTextJson/JsonCodec.cs.backup
@@ -0,0 +1,262 @@
+using System;
+using System.Buffers;
+using System.Collections.Generic;
+using System.Linq;
+using System.Reflection;
+using System.Text.Json;
+using System.Text.Json.Nodes;
+using Microsoft.Extensions.Options;
+using Orleans.Metadata;
+using Orleans.Serialization.Buffers;
+using Orleans.Serialization.Buffers.Adaptors;
+using Orleans.Serialization.Cloning;
+using Orleans.Serialization.Codecs;
+using Orleans.Serialization.Serializers;
+using Orleans.Serialization.WireProtocol;
+
+namespace Orleans.Serialization;
+
+/// <summary>
+/// A serialization codec which uses <see cref="JsonSerializer"/>.
+/// </summary>
+[Alias(WellKnownAlias)]
+public class JsonCodec : IGeneralizedCodec, IGeneralizedCopier, ITypeFilter
+{
+    private static readonly Type SelfType = typeof(JsonCodec);
+    private readonly ICodecSelector[] _serializableTypeSelectors;
+    private readonly ICopierSelector[] _copyableTypeSelectors;
+    private readonly JsonCodecOptions _options;
+
+    /// <summary>
+    /// The well-known type alias for this codec.
+    /// </summary>
+    public const string WellKnownAlias = "json";
+
+    /// <summary>
+    /// Initializes a new instance of the <see cref="JsonCodec"/> class.
+    /// </summary>
+    /// <param name="serializableTypeSelectors">Filters used to indicate which types should be serialized by this codec.</param>
+    /// <param name="copyableTypeSelectors">Filters used to indicate which types should be copied by this codec.</param>
+    /// <param name="options">The JSON codec options.</param>
+    public JsonCodec(
+        IEnumerable<ICodecSelector> serializableTypeSelectors,
+        IEnumerable<ICopierSelector> copyableTypeSelectors,
+        IOptions<JsonCodecOptions> options)
+    {
+        _serializableTypeSelectors = serializableTypeSelectors.Where(t => string.Equals(t.CodecName, WellKnownAlias, StringComparison.Ordinal)).ToArray();
+        _copyableTypeSelectors = copyableTypeSelectors.Where(t => string.Equals(t.CopierName, WellKnownAlias, StringComparison.Ordinal)).ToArray();
+        _options = options.Value;
+    }
+
+    /// <inheritdoc/>
+    void IFieldCodec.WriteField<TBufferWriter>(ref Writer<TBufferWriter> writer, uint fieldIdDelta, Type expectedType, object value)
+    {
+        if (ReferenceCodec.TryWriteReferenceField(ref writer, fieldIdDelta, expectedType, value))
+        {
+            return;
+        }
+
+        // The schema type when serializing the field is the type of the codec.
+        // In practice it could be any unique type as long as this codec is registered as the handler.
+        // By checking against the codec type in IsSupportedType, the codec could also just be registered as an IGenericCodec.
+        // Note that the codec is responsible for serializing the type of the value itself.
+        writer.WriteFieldHeader(fieldIdDelta, expectedType, SelfType, WireType.TagDelimited);
+
+        // Write the type name
+        ReferenceCodec.MarkValueField(writer.Session);
+        writer.WriteFieldHeaderExpected(0, WireType.LengthPrefixed);
+        writer.Session.TypeCodec.WriteLengthPrefixed(ref writer, value.GetType());
+
+        // Write the serialized payload
+        // Note that the Utf8JsonWriter and PooledBuffer could be pooled as long as they're correctly
+        // reset at the end of each use.
+        var bufferWriter = new BufferWriterBox<PooledBuffer>(new PooledBuffer());
+        try
+        {
+            var jsonWriter = new Utf8JsonWriter(bufferWriter);
+            JsonSerializer.Serialize(jsonWriter, value, _options.SerializerOptions);
+            jsonWriter.Flush();
+
+            ReferenceCodec.MarkValueField(writer.Session);
+            writer.WriteFieldHeaderExpected(1, WireType.LengthPrefixed);
+            writer.WriteVarUInt32((uint)bufferWriter.Value.Length);
+            bufferWriter.Value.CopyTo(ref writer);
+        }
+        finally
+        {
+            bufferWriter.Value.Dispose();
+        }
+
+        writer.WriteEndObject();
+    }
+
+    /// <inheritdoc/>
+    object IFieldCodec.ReadValue<TInput>(ref Reader<TInput> reader, Field field)
+    {
+        if (field.IsReference)
+        {
+            return ReferenceCodec.ReadReference(ref reader, field.FieldType);
+        }
+
+        field.EnsureWireTypeTagDelimited();
+
+        var placeholderReferenceId = ReferenceCodec.CreateRecordPlaceholder(reader.Session);
+        object result = null;
+        Type type = null;
+        uint fieldId = 0;
+        while (true)
+        {
+            var header = reader.ReadFieldHeader();
+            if (header.IsEndBaseOrEndObject)
+            {
+                break;
+            }
+
+            fieldId += header.FieldIdDelta;
+            switch (fieldId)
+            {
+                case 0:
+                    ReferenceCodec.MarkValueField(reader.Session);
+                    type = reader.Session.TypeCodec.ReadLengthPrefixed(ref reader);
+                    break;
+                case 1:
+                    if (type is null)
+                    {
+                        ThrowTypeFieldMissing();
+                    }
+
+                    ReferenceCodec.MarkValueField(reader.Session);
+                    var length = reader.ReadVarUInt32();
+
+                    // To possibly improve efficiency, this could be converted to read a ReadOnlySequence<byte> instead of a byte array.
+                    var tempBuffer = new PooledBuffer();
+                    try
+                    {
+                        reader.ReadBytes(ref tempBuffer, (int)length);
+                        var sequence = tempBuffer.AsReadOnlySequence();
+                        var jsonReader = new Utf8JsonReader(sequence, _options.ReaderOptions);
+                        result = JsonSerializer.Deserialize(ref jsonReader, type, _options.SerializerOptions);
+                    }
+                    finally
+                    {
+                        tempBuffer.Dispose();
+                    }
+
+                    break;
+                default:
+                    reader.ConsumeUnknownField(header);
+                    break;
+            }
+        }
+
+        ReferenceCodec.RecordObject(reader.Session, result, placeholderReferenceId);
+        return result;
+    }
+
+    /// <inheritdoc/>
+    bool IGeneralizedCodec.IsSupportedType(Type type)
+    {
+        if (type == SelfType)
+        {
+            return true;
+        }
+
+        if (CommonCodecTypeFilter.IsAbstractOrFrameworkType(type))
+        {
+            return false;
+        }
+
+        if (IsNativelySupportedType(type))
+        {
+            return true;
+        }
+
+        foreach (var selector in _serializableTypeSelectors)
+        {
+            if (selector.IsSupportedType(type))
+            {
+                return true;
+            }
+        }
+
+        if (_options.IsSerializableType?.Invoke(type) is bool value)
+        {
+            return value;
+        }
+
+        return false;
+    }
+
+    private static bool IsNativelySupportedType(Type type)
+    {
+        // Add types natively supported by System.Text.Json
+        // From https://github.com/dotnet/runtime/blob/2c4d0df3b146f8322f676b83a53ca21a065bdfc7/src/libraries/System.Text.Json/gen/JsonSourceGenerator.Parser.cs#L1792-L1797
+        return type == typeof(JsonArray)
+            || type == typeof(JsonElement)
+            || type == typeof(JsonObject)
+            || type == typeof(JsonDocument)
+            || typeof(JsonNode).IsAssignableFrom(type)
+            || typeof(JsonValue).IsAssignableFrom(type);
+    }
+
+    /// <inheritdoc/>
+    object IDeepCopier.DeepCopy(object input, CopyContext context)
+    {
+        if (context.TryGetCopy(input, out object result))
+            return result;
+
+
+        var bufferWriter = new BufferWriterBox<PooledBuffer>(new PooledBuffer());
+        try
+        {
+            var jsonWriter = new Utf8JsonWriter(bufferWriter);
+            JsonSerializer.Serialize(jsonWriter, input, _options.SerializerOptions);
+            jsonWriter.Flush();
+
+            var sequence = bufferWriter.Value.AsReadOnlySequence();
+            var jsonReader = new Utf8JsonReader(sequence, _options.ReaderOptions);
+            result = JsonSerializer.Deserialize(ref jsonReader, input.GetType(), _options.SerializerOptions);
+        }
+        finally
+        {
+            bufferWriter.Value.Dispose();
+        }
+
+        context.RecordCopy(input, result);
+        return result;
+    }
+
+    /// <inheritdoc/>
+    bool IGeneralizedCopier.IsSupportedType(Type type)
+    {
+        if (CommonCodecTypeFilter.IsAbstractOrFrameworkType(type))
+        {
+            return false;
+        }
+
+        if (IsNativelySupportedType(type))
+        {
+            return true;
+        }
+
+        foreach (var selector in _copyableTypeSelectors)
+        {
+            if (selector.IsSupportedType(type))
+            {
+                return true;
+            }
+        }
+
+        if (_options.IsCopyableType?.Invoke(type) is bool value)
+        {
+            return value;
+        }
+
+        return false;
+    }
+
+    /// <inheritdoc/>
+    bool? ITypeFilter.IsTypeAllowed(Type type) => (((IGeneralizedCopier)this).IsSupportedType(type) || ((IGeneralizedCodec)this).IsSupportedType(type)) ? true : null;
+
+    private static void ThrowTypeFieldMissing() => throw new RequiredFieldMissingException("Serialized value is missing its type field.");
+}
\ No newline at end of file
